      <div style="margin-left:1.6em; margin-top: 0.2em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;">
       <i>
        "Local chapter/s" redirects here. To see other possible uses, see
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Chapters" title="Special:MyLanguage/Chapters">
         Chapters
        </a>
        , a disambiguation page.
       </i>
      </div>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia">
        Wikimedia
       </a>
       chapters are independent organizations founded to support and promote the Wikimedia projects in a specified geographical region (in most cases, a country). Like the
       <a class="extiw" href="https://foundation.wikimedia.org/wiki/Home" title="foundation:Home">
        Wikimedia Foundation
       </a>
       , they aim to "empower and engage people around the world to collect and develop educational content under a free license or in the public domain, and to disseminate it effectively and globally". There are currently
       <b>
        39
       </b>
       chapters, with at least one on every inhabited continent.
      </p>
      <p>
       This page lists current and planned chapters. Please see the
       <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Step-by-step_chapter_creation_guide" title="Special:MyLanguage/Step-by-step chapter creation guide">
        step-by-step chapter creation guide
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Movement_affiliates_FAQ" title="Special:MyLanguage/Movement affiliates FAQ">
        movement affiliates FAQ
       </a>
       for more information. The
       <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations_Committee" title="Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations Committee">
        Affiliations Committee
       </a>
       advises on and assists the creation of and to support affiliates.
      </p>
      <p>
       Some chapters have an
       <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_offices" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia offices">
        office
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       <b>
        Find an overview of chapter-related Meta pages on
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Chapters_Portal" title="Special:MyLanguage/Chapters Portal">
         Chapters Portal
        </a>
        .
       </b>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tleft">

         Existing chapters, both founded (
         <b style="color:#008">
          dark blue
         </b>
         ) and approved (
         <b style="color:#068">
          dark turquoise
         </b>
         ), planned chapters (
         <b style="color:#0a8">
          green
         </b>
         ), and chapters in discussion (
         <b style="color:#0dd">
          light blue
         </b>
         ) as of 28 August 2019.
        </div>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" data-mw-comment='{"type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Existing_chapters","replies":[],"headingLevel":2,"placeholderHeading":false}' id="Existing_chapters">
        <span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Existing_chapters">
        </span>
        Existing chapters
        <span data-mw-comment-end="h-Existing_chapters">
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       There are currently
       <b>
        39
       </b>
       recognised Wikimedia chapters.
      </p>
      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" data-mw-comment='{"type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Chapters_in_discussion_phase","replies":[],"headingLevel":2,"placeholderHeading":false}' id="Chapters_in_discussion_phase">
        <span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Chapters_in_discussion_phase">
        </span>
        Chapters in discussion phase
        <span data-mw-comment-end="h-Chapters_in_discussion_phase">
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       <i>
        Chapters in active preparation to become a chapter. You should add here any chapter that is under discussion to be started up. Please provide link to a page (in meta) with more detailed information (at best with a short summary in English) and provide a contact for questions about the present state.
       </i>
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dt>
        Key
       </dt>
       <dd>
        A
        <span style="background:#FFC;padding:4px">
         yellowish
        </span>
        background means organizations are currently in active contact (as of the "last update" date) with the Affiliations Committee;
       </dd>
       <dd>
        A
        <span style="background:#EEE;padding:4px">
         light grey
        </span>
        background means awaiting an update (from the proposed organization? from AffCom?)
       </dd>
       <dd>
        A
        <span style="background:#CCF;padding:4px">
         light blue
        </span>
        background means the AffCom has asked the Board to approve the organization's formation.
       </dd>
      </dl>

          Wikimedia United States Coalition
         </a>
        </b>
        –
        <a class="external text" href="https://lists.wikimedia.org/mailman/listinfo/wikimediaus-l">
         mailing list
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Cascadia" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Cascadia">
          Wikimedia Cascadia
         </a>
        </b>
        – a chapter in the Pacific Northwest (Oregon and Washington and possibly including Northern California and/or British Columbia)
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a class="new" href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Florida" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Florida (page does not exist)">
          Wikimedia Florida
         </a>
        </b>
        – Possibility of a chapter for Florida
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Oklahoma" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Oklahoma">
          Wikimedia Oklahoma
         </a>
        </b>
        – Possibility of a chapter for Oklahoma
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a class="new" href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Texas" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Texas (page does not exist)">
          Wikimedia Texas
         </a>
        </b>
        – Possibility of a chapter for Texas and the south-central United States
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" data-mw-comment='{"type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-In_Asia-Ideas_for_chapters","replies":[],"headingLevel":3,"placeholderHeading":false}' id="In_Asia">
        <span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-In_Asia-Ideas_for_chapters">
        </span>
        In Asia
        <span data-mw-comment-end="h-In_Asia-Ideas_for_chapters">
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Mainland_China" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Mainland China">
          Wikimedia Mainland China
         </a>
        </b>
        – The discussion of establishing a chapter started in 2009 on
        <a class="extiw" href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E7%BB%B4%E5%9F%BA%E5%AA%92%E4%BD%93%E5%8D%8F%E4%BC%9A/%E7%AD%B9%E5%A4%87" title="zh:Wikipedia:中国维基媒体协会/筹备">
         Chinese Wikipedia
        </a>
        . The discussion was ended due to the political problems and no possibility of being legally incorporated. While the discussion restarted in 2013 when WMF start to recognize User Group, and the
        <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_User_Group_China" title="Wikimedia User Group China">
         Wikimedia User Group China
        </a>
        has been recognized since August 2014. There is no further plan for forming a chapter before the NPO can be freely incorporated in mainland China.
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Japan" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Japan">
          Wikimedia Japan
         </a>
        </b>
        – 設立の是非について投票中です。 The page reads "There are currently no active arguments to establish a local Japanese chapter, mainly because very few Japanese language community members are interested in it. Lack of legal knowledge and accounting skills among the community is also a large contributing factor."
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Nepal" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Nepal">
          Wikimedia Nepal
         </a>
        </b>
        <a class="extiw" href="https://ne.wikipedia.org/wiki/%E0%A4%B5%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%95%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%AA%E0%A5%80%E0%A4%A1%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%AF%E0%A4%BE:%E0%A4%B5%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%95%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%AE%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%A1%E0%A4%BF%E0%A4%AF%E0%A4%BE_%E0%A4%A8%E0%A5%87%E0%A4%AA%E0%A4%BE%E0%A4%B2" title="ne:विकिपीडिया:विकिमिडिया नेपाल">
         विकिमिडिया नेपाल
        </a>
        is recognized as a user group
        <b>
         Wikimedians of Nepal
        </b>
        on 29th May, 2013. Now it is in the way of becoming national chapter. Wikipedia was begun in Nepal on June 3, 2002 with Nepali Wikipedia. Now Wikipedias are avaible in five languages spoken in Nepal. Wikimedia Nepal begun regular meetups and discussions from 17 July 2010. It has been organizing outreach and various programs to promote Wikipedia in Nepal.
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Pakistan" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Pakistan">
          Wikimedia Pakistan
         </a>
        </b>
        is recognized as a user group.
       </li>
      </ul>

      </p>

       <li>

        </a>
        (Aegis Maelstrom), president
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="extiw" href="https://pl.wikipedia.org/wiki/chapter:U%C5%BCytkownik:WTM" title="pl:chapter:Użytkownik:WTM">

        </a>
        (WTM), treasurer
       </li>
       <li>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" data-mw-comment='{"type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Inter-chapter_initiatives","replies":[],"headingLevel":2,"placeholderHeading":false}' id="Inter-chapter_initiatives">
        <span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Inter-chapter_initiatives">
        </span>
        Inter-chapter initiatives
        <span data-mw-comment-end="h-Inter-chapter_initiatives">
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r19611965">
       .mw-parser-output .mw-tpl-seealso{font-style:italic;padding-bottom:0.4em;padding-left:0;margin-bottom:0.4em;margin-left:1em;color:#555;border-bottom:1px solid #ccc}
      </style>
      <div class="boilerplate seealso mw-tpl-seealso">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Interchapter_groups" title="Special:MyLanguage/Interchapter groups">
        Interchapter groups
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Active:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <i>
         Chapters Council
        </i>
        , a proposed central organization for chapters intended to promote coordination and accountability. See
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Chapters_Association" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Chapters Association">
         Wikimedia Chapters Association
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Iberocoop" title="Special:MyLanguage/Iberocoop">
          Regional Cooperation Initiative for Ibero-America (Iberocoop)
         </a>
        </b>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_United_States_Coalition" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia United States Coalition">
          Wikimedia United States Coalition
         </a>
        </b>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Central_and_Eastern_European_Wikimedia_Group" title="Special:MyLanguage/Central and Eastern European Wikimedia Group">
          Central and Eastern European Wikimedia Group
         </a>
        </b>
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Asia_Project" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Asia Project">
          Wikimedia Asia
         </a>
        </b>
        , a regional cooperation initiative for chapters and working groups in Asia and Australia.
       </li>
       <li>
        <b>
         <a href="/wiki/EU_policy" title="EU policy">
          Free Knowledge Advocacy Group EU
         </a>
        </b>
        , an initiative in the European Union to have a clear and coherent position on major legislative and political changes affecting the vision, mission and values of the Wikimedia movement.
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       Ideas:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/European_Wikimedia_chapter" title="Special:MyLanguage/European Wikimedia chapter">
         European Wikimedia chapter
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" data-mw-comment='{"type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Mailing_lists_and_wikis","replies":[],"headingLevel":2,"placeholderHeading":false}' id="Mailing_lists_and_wikis">
        <span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Mailing_lists_and_wikis">
        </span>
        Mailing lists and wikis
        <span data-mw-comment-end="h-Mailing_lists_and_wikis">
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       Apart from public
       <a href="/wiki/Mailing_lists" title="Mailing lists">
        mailing lists
       </a>
       (most notably
       <a class="extiw" href="https://lists.wikimedia.org/mailman/listinfo/Chapters-reports" title="mail:Chapters-reports">
        Chapters-reports
       </a>
       ) and websites listed elsewhere, there are two main private channels for communication and coordination among chapters, which existing chapters must follow and participate in:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Internal wiki
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">
         <a href="#cite_note-22">
          [22]
         </a>
        </sup>
        and
        <a class="extiw" href="https://lists.wikimedia.org/mailman/listinfo/Internal-l" title="mail:Internal-l">
         Internal-l – Local Chapters, board and officers coordination
        </a>
        : each chapter can subscribe an unlimited number of board members (as of 13th August 2010), with an e-mail to the list admin by the president; additional members can be subscribed following the usual procedure (endorsement by a subscribed person + consensus on wiki);
       </li>
       <li>
        Chapters wiki
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">
         <a href="#cite_note-23">
          [23]
         </a>
        </sup>
        and chapters mailinglist
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">
         <a href="#cite_note-24">
          [24]
         </a>
        </sup>
        for discussions and decisions among chapters: each chapter can subscribe unlimited board members (and some staffer) and an email by the president of the chapter to the
        <a class="external text" href="mailto:chapters-owner@wikimedia.ch" rel="nofollow">
         list admins
        </a>
        with the list of email addresses to add/remove is the usual process; there are also
        <a class="external text" href="https://intern.wikimedia.ch/lists/listinfo" rel="nofollow">
         other lists for working groups
        </a>
        , generally subsets of the previous one, apart some more open lists (e.g.
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/GLAM#See_also" title="Special:MyLanguage/GLAM">
         GLAM
        </a>
        ).
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" data-mw-comment='{"type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Wikimedia_chapters_related_news_and_announcements","replies":[],"headingLevel":2,"placeholderHeading":false}' id="Wikimedia_chapters_related_news_and_announcements">
        <span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Wikimedia_chapters_related_news_and_announcements">
        </span>
        Wikimedia chapters related news and announcements
        <span data-mw-comment-end="h-Wikimedia_chapters_related_news_and_announcements">
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <code>
         2014-07-27
        </code>
        Following a
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations_Committee/RFCs/Wikimedia_user_group_logos" title="Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations Committee/RFCs/Wikimedia user group logos">
         request for comments
        </a>
        , Affiliations Committee publishes
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_movement_affiliates_logos_best_practices" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia movement affiliates logos best practices">
         best practices guide for creation of Wikimedia movement affiliate logos
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         2014-06-23
        </code>
        <a href="/wiki/Affiliations_Committee/Resolutions/Wikimedia_Belgium_-_June_2014" title="Affiliations Committee/Resolutions/Wikimedia Belgium - June 2014">
         Affiliations Committee recommends
        </a>
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Foundation_Board_of_Trustees" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Foundation Board of Trustees">
         Wikimedia Foundation Board of Trustees
        </a>
        vote to recognize
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Belgium" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Belgium">
         Wikimedia Belgium
        </a>
        as a
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_chapters" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia chapters">
         Wikimedia chapter
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         2013-11-25
        </code>
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations_Committee/Resolutions/Wikimedia_Iceland" title="Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations Committee/Resolutions/Wikimedia Iceland">
         Recommendation to the Board to recognise Wikimedia Iceland as a chapter
        </a>
        . The board decided not to do so.
       </li>
       <li>
        <code>
         2013-07-12
        </code>
        Based on
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations_Committee/Resolutions/Wikimedia_Uruguay_%E2%80%93_June_2013" title="Special:MyLanguage/Affiliations Committee/Resolutions/Wikimedia Uruguay – June 2013">
         advice provided
        </a>
        by the Affiliations Committee,
        <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Uruguay" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Uruguay">
         Wikimedia Uruguay
        </a>
        has been
        <a class="extiw" href="https://foundation.wikimedia.org/wiki/Resolution:Recognition_of_Wikimedia_Uruguay" title="wmf:Resolution:Recognition of Wikimedia Uruguay">
         recognized
        </a>
        as a chapter.
       </li>
       <li>
        <small>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_chapters/News" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia chapters/News">
          Other news and archives...
         </a>
        </small>
       </li>
      </ul>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" data-mw-comment='{"type":"heading","level":0,"id":"h-Notes","replies":[],"headingLevel":2,"placeholderHeading":false}' id="Notes">

        Notes
        <span data-mw-comment-end="h-Notes">
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns">
       <ol class="references">
        <li id="cite_note-1">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <a href="#cite_ref-1">
           ↑
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="reference-text">
          Is the chapter formally recognized as a
          <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:Nonprofit_organization" title="w:en:Nonprofit organization">
           Nonprofit organization
          </a>
          under its nation's laws? "n/a" should be used if the country's laws do not recognize a nonprofit status.
         </span>
        </li>
        <li id="cite_note-2">
         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
          <a href="#cite_ref-2">

          <a class="external autonumber" href="http://www.cagi.ch/en/service-ong/creation-transfert/creation-dune-association.php" rel="nofollow">
           [1]
          </a>
          <a class="external autonumber" href="http://www.cagi.ch/en/service-ong/modele-de-statuts.php" rel="nofollow">
           [2]
          </a>
          . The tax exemption has been formally approved
          <a class="external autonumber" href="http://members.wikimedia.ch/Tax" rel="nofollow">
           [3]
          </a>
          .
         </span>

Wikimédia Magyarország is recognized as "organization for the public benefit" status which means: transparency requirements, tax exemptions, tax deductibility etc.
